<Z>Gameplan Baseball Changes <C> Most leagues have now moved up to 2024 rules, or are getting close. These changes are to improve <L.31.1>
the financial balance of the game, make it somewhat more even and provide you with a few more options and decisions. For Gameplan <L.31.1>
Baseball I've got a webpage with the changes, which you can find at www.pbmsports.com/baseball2024.htm (note it is case sensitive). <L.31.1>
These will generally come into play at the start of a new season, but most actually impact at the end of the season. I will review <L.31.1>
them in the autumn, but don't expect any changes until then, and with other things (see above) taking my focus. <L.31.1>

If you get it wrong, there's a risk the turn gets missed. Please also avoid double submission of turns - if they're within minutes<L.31.1>
the system will only take the latest set, but if they're spread out both may be input and you'll get charged 0.1 credit.<L.31.1>
